##### **EnTrust: Modeling Inter-Modal Conflict for Trustworthy Multimodal Medical Image Analysis**
2606.21384v1 by Dwarikanath Mahapatra, Abhijit Das, Behzad Bozorgtabar, Zongyuan Ge, Sudipta Roy, Deepak Nayak, Mauricio Reyes, Imran Razzak

Multimodal medical imaging fuses complementary anatomical and functional information, yet modalities frequently disagree in pathologically heterogeneous regions. Current segmentation models handle this in one of two inadequate ways: deterministic fusion that averages away disagreement, or post-hoc uncertainty estimation decoupled from the fusion process that produces it. Both obscure the clinically critical question: why is this prediction unreliable? We present EnTrust, a framework that treats inter-modal conflict as the primary source of predictive uncertainty. Our EnFuse module decomposes multimodal features into three disentangled components: shared anatomical consensus (F_c), modality-specific cues (F_{u,m}), and spatially localized conflict signals (F_{cf}), with independence enforced via a cross-covariance objective. This structured decomposition conditions SegDiff, a diffusion-based generative segmentation model whose sampled hypotheses diverge specifically in regions of modal disagreement. TrustMap then translates this hypothesis divergence into calibrated, pixel-wise uncertainty using ensemble entropy, conflict-guided perturbation probing, and a learned calibration head, enabling clinicians to understand not only where predictions are uncertain, but why. Across four benchmarks spanning brain, cardiac, lesion, and oncology domains, EnTrust achieves state-of-the-art segmentation accuracy while reducing calibration error by 40% compared to the strongest baseline. Notably, it outperforms 5x deep ensembles using a single model at roughly half the memory footprint. Code and checkpoints are available at https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/EnTrust.git.

摘要：多模態醫學影像融合了互補的解剖和功能信息，但在病理異質性區域，模態之間經常存在不一致。目前的分割模型以兩種不充分的方式處理這一問題：確定性融合通過平均消除不一致，或與生成過程解耦的事後不確定性估計。這兩者都掩蓋了臨床上關鍵的問題：為什麼這個預測不可靠？我們提出了 EnTrust，一個將模態間衝突視為預測不確定性主要來源的框架。我們的 EnFuse 模塊將多模態特徵分解為三個獨立的組件：共享的解剖共識 (F_c)、模態特定的線索 (F_{u,m}) 和空間定位的衝突信號 (F_{cf})，並通過交叉協方差目標強制獨立性。這一結構化分解為 SegDiff 提供了條件，SegDiff 是一個基於擴散的生成分割模型，其樣本假設在模態不一致的區域特別發散。然後，TrustMap 將這一假設的發散轉化為經過校準的逐像素不確定性，使用集成熵、衝突引導的擾動探測和學習的校準頭，使臨床醫生不僅能理解預測在哪裡不確定，還能理解為什麼不確定。在涵蓋大腦、心臟、病變和肿瘤學領域的四個基準測試中，EnTrust 實現了最先進的分割準確性，同時將校準誤差減少了 40%，相比於最強的基準值得到的結果。值得注意的是，它在大約一半的內存占用下，使用單一模型超越了 5 倍的深度集成。代碼和檢查點可在 https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/EnTrust.git 獲得。

##### **Graph-of-Differences: Anatomy-Structured Difference Alignment for Medical Image Re-Identification**
2606.21368v1 by Nichula Wasalathilaka, Abhijit Das, Imran Razzak, Dwarikanath Mahapatra

Medical image re-identification (MedReID) enables longitudinal patient linkage but remains vulnerable to shortcut learning and often produces decisions that clinicians cannot audit against named anatomy. We propose Graph-of-Differences (GoD), which grounds identity comparisons in explicit anatomical structure. Each image is represented as an anatomy graph whose nodes correspond to named anatomical regions; given an image pair, soft node correspondence is established, and differences are computed over matched anatomy. A graph-level difference alignment objective ties these anatomy-matched differences to the global backbone difference, ensuring the retrieval signal is anchored in homologous structures rather than arbitrary spatial tokens. Explanations are defined over named graph nodes and quantitatively audited via node insertion/deletion tests, replacing unstable pixel heatmaps with verifiable structure-level evidence. On internal benchmarks, GoD improves Rank-1 by +7.1 pp on fundus and +3.1 pp on CXR over a strong frozen-backbone baseline, with further gains on zero-shot external transfers confirming that anatomy grounding improves both accuracy and generalization. Code is available at https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/GoD.git.

摘要：醫學影像重識別（MedReID）使得長期患者連結成為可能，但仍然容易受到捷徑學習的影響，並且經常產生臨床醫生無法根據命名解剖學進行審核的決策。我們提出了差異圖（GoD），它將身份比較基於明確的解剖結構。每個影像都被表示為一個解剖圖，其節點對應於命名的解剖區域；給定一對影像，建立軟節點對應，並計算匹配解剖上的差異。一個圖層級的差異對齊目標將這些解剖匹配的差異與全局骨幹差異相連，確保檢索信號基於同源結構而非任意空間標記。解釋是基於命名圖節點定義的，並通過節點插入/刪除測試進行定量審核，取代不穩定的像素熱圖，提供可驗證的結構層級證據。在內部基準測試中，GoD在強大的凍結骨幹基線上，對眼底影像提高了+7.1個百分點，對胸部X光影像提高了+3.1個百分點，並且在零樣本外部轉移中進一步獲得增益，證實了解剖學基礎改善了準確性和泛化能力。代碼可在 https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/GoD.git 獲得。

##### **Towards Dys-XAI: Influence-Based Explanations for Dysarthria Severity Assessment**
2606.21306v1 by Xiaoliang Wu, Qiyang Sun, Yupei Li, Erfan Loweimi, Jennifer Williams, Zhengjun Yue

Dysarthria severity assessment is essential for therapy planning and longitudinal monitoring, yet manual perceptual rating is time-consuming and variable across clinicians. Although deep learning models achieve strong performance, their black-box nature limits clinical adoption. Existing speech explainability methods typically provide acoustic feature importance scores that are difficult for end-users to interpret. We propose an influence-based, instance-level explainability framework that explains each decision through supportive and competing training samples. Using gradient-based influence approximations, we compute per-utterance influence scores to identify supportive and competing training samples for each prediction. Controlled deletion experiments from 5 to 20 percent validate the explanations, showing that removing highly influential samples systematically shifts predictions. This approach provides auditable explanations by linking decisions to perceptible reference cases.

摘要：語音障礙的嚴重程度評估對於治療計劃和長期監測至關重要，然而手動感知評分既耗時又因臨床醫生而異。雖然深度學習模型表現出色，但其黑箱特性限制了臨床應用。現有的語音可解釋性方法通常提供難以讓最終用戶解釋的聲學特徵重要性分數。我們提出了一種基於影響的實例級可解釋性框架，通過支持性和競爭性訓練樣本來解釋每個決策。使用基於梯度的影響近似，我們計算每次發話的影響分數，以識別每個預測的支持性和競爭性訓練樣本。從5%到20%的控制刪除實驗驗證了解釋，顯示移除高度影響樣本會系統性地改變預測。這種方法通過將決策與可感知的參考案例聯繫起來，提供可審計的解釋。

##### **Few-Shot Hyperspectral Aphid Detection via FastGAN Synthetic Data Generation, Transformer-Based Classification and Explainable AI**
2606.21267v1 by Ali Saeidan

Early detection of aphid infestation in crops is essential for preventing yield loss and reducing unnecessary pesticide use. Hyperspectral imaging combined with Spectral Information Divergence (SID) analysis offers a non-destructive approach for monitoring plant health; however, deep learning methods applied to hyperspectral data are often limited by small dataset sizes. In this study, a data-efficient generative adversarial network (FastGAN) was employed to augment a hyperspectral SID dataset of faba bean leaves containing healthy and aphid-infested samples. The trained generator produced 10,000 synthetic images preserving structural and spectral characteristics of real samples. Image quality was evaluated using Frechet Inception Distance (FID), demonstrating stable convergence and realistic reconstruction of leaf morphology and infestation patterns. The augmented dataset was used to train four classification architectures: VGG16, ResNet-50, EfficientNet, and Vision Transformer (ViT). Results showed that dataset augmentation significantly improved classification robustness, with performance progressively increasing from classical convolutional networks to transformer-based models. The ViT model achieved the highest accuracy and F1-scores, while EfficientNet provided strong balanced performance and ResNet-50 showed moderate improvements over VGG16. Confusion matrix analysis confirmed reduced false negatives and improved disease detection when using advanced architectures. The findings demonstrate that FastGAN-based augmentation effectively enhances hyperspectral plant disease classification and that transformer-based models provide the most reliable discrimination between healthy and infested leaves.

摘要：早期檢測作物中的蚜蟲侵害對於防止產量損失和減少不必要的農藥使用至關重要。高光譜成像結合光譜信息差異（SID）分析提供了一種無損的方法來監測植物健康；然而，應用於高光譜數據的深度學習方法通常受到小數據集大小的限制。在本研究中，採用了數據高效的生成對抗網絡（FastGAN）來增強包含健康和蚜蟲侵害樣本的蠶豆葉高光譜SID數據集。訓練後的生成器生成了10,000張合成圖像，保留了真實樣本的結構和光譜特徵。圖像質量使用Frechet Inception Distance（FID）進行評估，顯示出穩定的收斂和葉片形態及侵害模式的真實重建。增強後的數據集用於訓練四種分類架構：VGG16、ResNet-50、EfficientNet和Vision Transformer（ViT）。結果顯示，數據集增強顯著提高了分類的穩健性，從傳統卷積網絡到基於Transformer的模型，性能逐步提高。ViT模型達到了最高的準確率和F1分數，而EfficientNet則提供了強勁的平衡性能，ResNet-50相對於VGG16顯示出適度的改進。混淆矩陣分析確認在使用先進架構時，假陰性減少，疾病檢測改善。研究結果表明，基於FastGAN的增強有效提升了高光譜植物疾病分類，而基於Transformer的模型提供了最可靠的健康與侵害葉片之間的區分。

##### **MEDLAYXPLAIN: Benchmarking the Expert-Lay Gap in Medical Vision-Language Models**
2606.21194v1 by Han Jang, Junhyeok Lee, Songsoo Kim, Chae Young Lim, Hyeonjin Goh, Heeseong Eum, Kyu Sung Choi

Medical Vision-Language Models (Med-VLMs) achieve strong expert-level performance, yet their ability to generate patient-accessible descriptions remains underexplored. With the 21st Century Cures Act now mandating immediate patient access to diagnostic imaging results, evaluating whether Med-VLMs can bridge this Expert-Lay Gap is both urgent and clinically consequential for patient education and shared decision-making. To this end, we introduce MedLayXPlain, the first large-scale multimodal benchmark and evaluation framework for Medical Lay Language Generation (MLLG). MedLayXPlain-122K provides 122,789 region-grounded samples across 8 imaging modalities from 12 publicly available source datasets, each comprising a medical image with paired expert and lay captions anchored in a three-level Unified Medical Language System (UMLS) ontology hierarchy spanning 7 semantic groups, 43 semantic types, and 2,411 medical concepts. Lay captions are constructed via Hierarchical Ontology-Verified Refinement (HOVER), a three-step pipeline combining patient-centric vocabulary mapping, LLM-based constrained rewriting, and cross-model visual verification to enforce semantic equivalence while preventing hallucination. We further introduce MedLayEval, a lightweight 3B evaluator distilled from a 27B verifier that scores expert-lay alignment across five clinically grounded attributes, addressing the poor correlation between standard NLG metrics and clinical judgment. Benchmarking 33 VLMs on MedLayXPlain-122K reveals a systematic Expert-Lay Gap: medical VLMs achieve strong expert captioning but suffer significant lay-register degradation, while general-purpose VLMs produce more accessible language yet lack clinical precision, confirming that neither current paradigm adequately serves patient-facing communication.

摘要：醫療視覺語言模型（Med-VLMs）達到了強大的專家級表現，但它們生成患者可接觸描述的能力仍然未被充分探索。隨著21世紀治療法案現在要求立即讓患者獲得診斷影像結果，評估Med-VLMs是否能夠彌合這一專家與普通人之間的差距對於患者教育和共同決策既緊迫又具有臨床意義。為此，我們介紹MedLayXPlain，首個大規模多模態基準和醫療通俗語言生成（MLLG）評估框架。MedLayXPlain-122K提供了來自12個公開可用源數據集的122,789個區域基礎樣本，涵蓋8種影像模態，每個樣本包括一幅醫療影像及其配對的專家和通俗標題，這些標題依託於一個三層的統一醫學語言系統（UMLS）本體層級，涵蓋7個語義組、43個語義類型和2,411個醫學概念。通俗標題是通過分層本體驗證精煉（HOVER）構建的，這是一個三步驟的流程，結合了以患者為中心的詞彙映射、基於LLM的約束重寫和跨模型視覺驗證，以強化語義等價性，同時防止幻覺。我們進一步介紹MedLayEval，這是一個從27B驗證器提煉而來的輕量級3B評估器，對五個臨床基礎屬性進行專家與通俗對齊的評分，解決了標準NLG指標與臨床判斷之間的低相關性。在MedLayXPlain-122K上對33個VLM進行基準測試顯示出系統性的專家與普通人之間的差距：醫療VLM在專家標題生成上表現強勁，但在通俗語言的使用上卻遭遇了顯著的退化，而通用VLM則產生了更易於理解的語言，但缺乏臨床精確性，這確認了目前的兩種範式都無法充分滿足面向患者的溝通需求。

##### **Anatomically Consistent TMJ Disc Segmentation via Semantic Anchoring and Clinical Priors**
2606.21177v1 by Dayun Ju, Chanyoung Kim, Sunyoung Jung, Hyo-Jung Jung, Chena Lee, Younjung Park, Seong Jae Hwang

Segmenting the temporomandibular joint (TMJ) disc from MRI is essential for accurate diagnosis of internal derangement, yet it remains unreliable in practice due to its small size, low contrast, and morphological variability. Existing methods, primarily adapted from general segmentation architectures, often produce fragmented or anatomically inconsistent masks, leading to unstable measurements of disc position and shape for downstream diagnosis. To address these challenges, we propose TISC, a TMJ disc segmentation framework that integrates semantic anchoring with clinical metadata-guided boundary refinement. The framework first establishes robust disc localization in the foundation model feature space via a Prototypical Semantic Anchoring (PSA) module that aggregates adjacent-slice MedDINOv3 features and derives a prototype-driven similarity map. It then performs targeted boundary refinement through a Clinical-Metadata Point Refinement (C-MPR) module, with point-wise predictions modulated by Mouth Open Limitation (MOL), a clinical indicator associated with disc displacement without reduction. On a large-scale cohort of 2,488 PD MRI volumes from 1,300 patients, our method achieves up to a 4.96 Dice improvement over strong baselines across diverse architectures, delivering more anatomically coherent and clinically reliable TMJ disc segmentation.

摘要：對於準確診斷內部損傷，從 MRI 中分割顳下頜關節 (TMJ) 磁碟是至關重要的，然而由於其小尺寸、低對比度和形態變異性，實際應用中仍然不可靠。現有的方法主要是從一般分割架構中改編而來，經常產生破碎或解剖學上不一致的面具，導致下游診斷中磁碟位置和形狀的測量不穩定。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了 TISC，一個 TMJ 磁碟分割框架，將語義錨定與臨床元數據引導的邊界細化相結合。該框架首先通過原型語義錨定 (PSA) 模塊，在基礎模型特徵空間中建立穩健的磁碟定位，該模塊聚合相鄰切片的 MedDINOv3 特徵並推導出原型驅動的相似性圖。然後，它通過臨床元數據點細化 (C-MPR) 模塊執行針對性的邊界細化，點對點的預測受到與無減少的磁碟位移相關的臨床指標——口腔開啟限制 (MOL) 的調節。在來自 1,300 名患者的 2,488 個 PD MRI 體積的大型隊列中，我們的方法在各種架構上實現了高達 4.96 的 Dice 改進，超越了強基準，提供了更具解剖一致性和臨床可靠性的 TMJ 磁碟分割。

##### **AdaMem: Learning What to Remember for Personalized Long-Horizon LLM Agents**
2606.21144v1 by Xingyu Chen, Rui Wang, Zhaopeng Tu, Liefeng Bo

Long-term memory systems for Large Language Model (LLM) agents typically try to \emph{remember everything}, extracting memories uniformly to retain as many facts as possible. In production, however, inference cost and finite context budgets make this untenable: beyond consolidating raw dialogue into memory, an agent must exert \emph{write control}, efficiently keeping only the information each user actually cares about. Otherwise, long-horizon personalized interactions suffer \emph{memory bloat}, where irrelevant trivia crowds out useful information and steadily erodes question-answering (QA) accuracy. We argue that what is worth remembering is role-dependent, and propose \textbf{AdaMem} (Adaptive Memory), a method that \emph{learns what to remember} for each user from feedback. AdaMem maintains a structured, role-specific Memory Policy and refines it from weekly QA feedback through a lightweight, patch-style self-reflection step with failure rollback. To study this setting, we build \textbf{AdaMem-Bench}, a benchmark that simulates weeks of interaction with week-by-week QA. Across two extraction models and two feedback modes, AdaMem improves QA accuracy by up to \textbf{+9.0\%} over the uniform Mem0 baseline while shrinking memory volume by \textbf{9\%}.

摘要：長期記憶系統對於大型語言模型（LLM）代理通常試圖\emph{記住所有事物}，均勻地提取記憶以保留盡可能多的事實。然而，在實際應用中，推理成本和有限的上下文預算使這變得不可行：除了將原始對話整合到記憶中，代理還必須施加\emph{寫入控制}，有效地僅保留每個用戶實際關心的信息。否則，長期個性化互動會遭受\emph{記憶膨脹}，無關的瑣事會擠占有用信息，並穩步侵蝕問答（QA）準確性。我們認為，值得記住的內容是依賴於角色的，並提出\textbf{AdaMem}（自適應記憶），這是一種\emph{學習記住什麼}的每個用戶的反饋方法。AdaMem維護一個結構化的、特定角色的記憶政策，並通過每週的QA反饋進行精煉，使用輕量級的、補丁式的自我反思步驟，並具有失敗回滾功能。為了研究這一設定，我們建立了\textbf{AdaMem-Bench}，這是一個基準，模擬了幾週的互動，並逐週進行QA。在兩個提取模型和兩個反饋模式下，AdaMem將QA準確性提高了最多\textbf{+9.0\%}，同時將記憶量縮減了\textbf{9\%}。

##### **Answer Engineering: Local Trajectory Editing for Protocol-Constrained Decision Making in Large Language Models**
2606.21121v1 by Victor Lavrenko, Anastasiia Molodnitskaia

Large language models can produce confident but protocol-invalid answers in domains where procedural compliance is critical. This paper presents Answer Engineering, a deterministic runtime and authoring layer that applies localized rule-guided interventions to the visible reasoning trajectory during standard autoregressive generation, without retraining, modifying model weights, or performing global search. The method is evaluated on a controlled clinical benchmark for sudden sensorineural hearing loss (SSNHL), where correct management depends on protocol-consistent interpretation of symptom timing, Weber/Rinne tuning-fork findings, and otoscopic findings. In the benchmark, step-by-step reasoning shifted rather than eliminated errors: compliant outcomes for SSNHL decreased from 54.5% under unguided generation to 25.1%, while acceptance on the conductive contrast condition increased from 1.6% to 58.9%. Local trajectory editing increased SSNHL compliance to 83.5% and conductive-case adherence to 77.9%, raising balanced accuracy from 42.0% under reasoning-only generation to 80.7%. The results support a systems-level view in which protocol adherence can be improved through auditable runtime control of reasoning trajectories, while also identifying limitations caused by rule coverage, trigger reliability, and persistent diagnosis-first generation dynamics.

摘要：大型語言模型在程序遵循至關重要的領域中可能會產生自信但不符合協議的答案。本文提出了答案工程，一種確定性的運行時和創作層，該層在標準自回歸生成過程中對可見的推理軌跡應用局部的規則指導干預，而無需重新訓練、修改模型權重或執行全局搜索。該方法在針對突發性感音神經性聽力損失（SSNHL）的受控臨床基準上進行評估，其中正確的管理依賴於對症狀時間、韋伯/林納音叉檢查結果和耳鏡檢查結果的協議一致解釋。在基準測試中，逐步推理改變而非消除錯誤：在未指導生成的情況下，SSNHL的合規結果從54.5%下降至25.1%，而在傳導對比條件下的接受率則從1.6%上升至58.9%。局部軌跡編輯將SSNHL的合規性提高至83.5%，而傳導案例的遵循率提高至77.9%，使得在僅依賴推理生成的情況下，平衡準確率從42.0%上升至80.7%。這些結果支持了一種系統層面的觀點，即通過可審計的運行時控制推理軌跡可以改善協議遵循，同時也識別出由於規則覆蓋、觸發可靠性和持續的診斷優先生成動態所造成的限制。

##### **MS-rPPG: Multi-spectral State Space Model for Remote Photoplethysmography in Driver Monitoring Systems**
2606.21115v1 by Jiho Choi, Sang Jun Lee

Remote photoplethysmography (rPPG) is a camera-based technique for measuring physiological signals, particularly cardiac activity. From the remotely measured signals, heart rate can be estimated, which is crucial for health monitoring. In this study, we investigate a driver health monitoring system based on remote heart rate estimation. However, driving environments represent uncontrolled settings where videos are subject to varying illumination conditions and frequent head movements. We introduce MS-rPPG, a multi-spectral framework that combines RGB with near-infrared (NIR) face video to alleviate rPPG estimation under challenging driving conditions. To combine the complementary features from two spectral videos, we propose a cross-spectral linear modulation (CSLM) strategy based on frequency-domain analysis. Moreover, we introduce MS-Mamba, a novel state space model designed to effectively model long-range temporal dependencies while jointly capturing cross-channel interactions between multi-spectral features. We collected a real-world dataset called MS-Drive, which was recorded from 50 participants while driving the vehicle. The proposed method was evaluated on the MR-NIRP Car dataset and MS-Drive datasets. The experimental results indicate that MS-rPPG shows better robustness and heart rate estimation accuracy than previous methods, highlighting its promise for driver health monitoring. The codes are available at github.com/ziiho08/MS-rPPG.

摘要：遠程光電容積描記法（rPPG）是一種基於攝影機的技術，用於測量生理信號，特別是心臟活動。從遠程測量的信號中，可以估算心率，這對健康監測至關重要。在本研究中，我們探討了一種基於遠程心率估算的駕駛員健康監測系統。然而，駕駛環境代表著不受控制的環境，視頻受到變化的照明條件和頻繁的頭部運動的影響。我們引入了MS-rPPG，一種多光譜框架，將RGB與近紅外（NIR）面部視頻結合，以減輕在挑戰性駕駛條件下的rPPG估算。為了結合兩個光譜視頻的互補特徵，我們提出了一種基於頻域分析的交叉光譜線性調製（CSLM）策略。此外，我們介紹了MS-Mamba，一種新穎的狀態空間模型，旨在有效建模長期時間依賴性，同時共同捕捉多光譜特徵之間的交叉通道交互。我們收集了一個名為MS-Drive的真實世界數據集，該數據集是從50名參與者駕駛汽車時錄製的。所提出的方法在MR-NIRP Car數據集和MS-Drive數據集上進行了評估。實驗結果表明，MS-rPPG顯示出比以往方法更好的穩健性和心率估算準確性，突顯了其在駕駛員健康監測中的潛力。代碼可在github.com/ziiho08/MS-rPPG獲得。

##### **CheXpercept: A Benchmark for Evaluating Expert-Level Lesion Perception in Chest X-rays**
2606.21020v1 by Geon Choi, Hangyul Yoon, Nalee Kim, Jeong Yun Jang, Hyunju Shin, Hyunki Park, Sang Hoon Seo, Edward Choi

The evaluation of vision-language models (VLMs) for chest X-ray (CXR) analysis has largely been limited to disease-presence classification without visual grounding. Such evaluations fail to verify the expert-level lesion perception necessary to ensure the clinical reliability of VLMs. To address these limitations, we introduce CheXpercept, a sequential, multi-level perception benchmark that mirrors a radiologist's cognitive workflow across coarse-level detection, fine-level contour evaluation and revision, and semantic-level attribute extraction. To ensure high clinical fidelity at scale, we construct the dataset using a semi-automated generation pipeline paired with a review by six medical experts. CheXpercept contains 10,400 QA items derived from 2,100 CXRs, covering seven clinically critical pulmonary and cardiac lesions. To demonstrate the current landscape of VLM perception, we benchmark 14 general and medical VLMs on CheXpercept. The models achieve adequate performance only at the coarse level, with accuracy degrading precipitously on deeper visual tasks. Notably, medical VLMs show almost no perceptual advantage over their general-domain counterparts, highlighting a systemic flaw in current domain adaptation. The code and dataset will be publicly available.

摘要：視覺-語言模型 (VLMs) 在胸部 X 光片 (CXR) 分析的評估大多僅限於疾病存在的分類，且未進行視覺基礎的驗證。這樣的評估未能驗證專家級的病變感知，這對於確保 VLMs 的臨床可靠性是必要的。為了解決這些限制，我們推出了 CheXpercept，一個序列式的多層次感知基準，模擬放射科醫生在粗略檢測、細緻輪廓評估和修訂以及語義層次屬性提取過程中的認知工作流程。為了確保在大規模下的高臨床真實性，我們使用半自動生成管道構建數據集，並由六位醫學專家進行審核。CheXpercept 包含 10,400 個來自 2,100 份 CXR 的 QA 項目，涵蓋七種臨床關鍵的肺部和心臟病變。為了展示當前 VLM 感知的現狀，我們在 CheXpercept 上對 14 個通用和醫學 VLM 進行基準測試。這些模型僅在粗略層次上達到適當的性能，並且在更深層次的視覺任務中準確率急劇下降。值得注意的是，醫學 VLM 幾乎沒有相對於其通用領域對應物的感知優勢，突顯了當前領域適應中的系統性缺陷。代碼和數據集將公開提供。

##### **Detecting Satellites in Radio-Frequency Data via Semi-Supervised Learning**
2606.20976v1 by Cade W. Trotter, Maksim E. Eren, Justin C. Holmes, J. Brent Parham, David Ewing, Boian S. Alexandrov, Gian Luca Delzanno

Radio-frequency (RF) monitoring is essential for space domain awareness, but it often generates large, variable, and sparsely populated datasets with few labels. These observations can capture satellites, space debris, and the ionospheric background, yet interpreting them typically requires specialized subject-matter expertise. Supervised deep learning methods can perform well on labeled RF data, but they require many annotated examples and may need careful retraining as RF conditions change. Semi-supervised approaches offer a practical alternative for limited-data settings by using unlabeled observations to reveal latent patterns that experts can interpret. In this paper, we present a semi-supervised RF detection and classification workflow for satellite monitoring that combines Non-negative Matrix Factorization with automatic model determination (NMFk), expert-guided cluster interpretation, and classifier-based prediction. We first represent RF observations as a non-negative feature matrix and apply NMFk to estimate the number of clusters that best captures patterns in the unlabeled data. Subject-matter experts then assign physical meaning to the resulting clusters, including satellite detections, ionospheric environmental conditions, and other RF event categories. Finally, we train a classifier on these interpreted clusters to evaluate performance on a test set and categorize future observations. This pipeline reduces reliance on large pre-labeled datasets by pairing unsupervised factorization with expert interpretation, enabling an interpretable and transferable methodology for detecting, observing, and classifying behavior in RF data.

摘要：無線頻率（RF）監測對於太空領域的認知至關重要，但它通常會產生大量、變化多端且稀疏的數據集，且標籤較少。這些觀測可以捕捉衛星、太空垃圾和電離層背景，但解釋這些數據通常需要專業的主題知識。監督式深度學習方法在標記的RF數據上表現良好，但它們需要大量的標註範例，並且可能需要在RF條件變化時進行仔細的重新訓練。半監督方法通過使用未標記的觀測來揭示專家可以解釋的潛在模式，為有限數據的情境提供了一個實用的替代方案。在本文中，我們提出了一種半監督RF檢測和分類工作流程，用於衛星監測，該流程結合了非負矩陣分解與自動模型確定（NMFk）、專家引導的聚類解釋和基於分類器的預測。我們首先將RF觀測表示為非負特徵矩陣，並應用NMFk來估計最佳捕捉未標記數據中模式的聚類數。然後，主題專家為所得到的聚類賦予物理意義，包括衛星檢測、電離層環境條件和其他RF事件類別。最後，我們在這些解釋過的聚類上訓練一個分類器，以評估在測試集上的性能並對未來觀測進行分類。這個流程通過將無監督分解與專家解釋相結合，減少了對大型預標記數據集的依賴，從而實現了一種可解釋且可轉移的方法論，用於檢測、觀測和分類RF數據中的行為。

##### **PROTON: Prototype-Based Test-Time Online OOD Detection for Medical VLMs**
2606.20913v1 by Abhijit Das, Nichula Wasalathilaka, Yifan Lu, Adinath Dukre, Dwarikanath Mahapatra, Shadab Khan, Imran Razzak

Medical vision-language models (VLMs) enable zero-shot clinical image classification, yet reliably detecting out-of-distribution (OOD) inputs at deployment remains an open problem. No static scoring method works across all shift types: Maximum Concept Matching (MCM) on FLAIR achieves 76.4% AUROC for far-OOD but only 42.4% for covariate shifts such as ultra-wide-field fundus images, effectively random. We trace this to a structural mismatch: covariate-shifted inputs are indistinguishable from in-distribution samples in softmax space, yet occupy distinct regions in the VLM embedding space. To exploit this untapped signal, we propose PROTON (PROtotype-based Test-time ONline OOD detection), a lightweight post-hoc module that maintains an online prototype bank from high-confidence test predictions and adaptively fuses prototype distance with MCM scoring via stream-level variance statistics, requiring no model modification, training data, or prompt engineering. On the ophthalmology benchmark FLAIR + FIVES, PROTON improves MCM by +23.9 AUROC on covariate shift, +8.8 on semantic shift, and +8.1 on far-OOD, making it the only zero-shot method to improve all three without hierarchical prompts or labeled data. Code is available at https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/PROTON, and the project page is available at https://genmi-lab.github.io/PROTON.

摘要：醫學視覺語言模型（VLMs）使得零樣本臨床影像分類成為可能，但在部署時可靠地檢測分佈外（OOD）輸入仍然是一個未解決的問題。沒有靜態評分方法能夠適用於所有類型的變化：在 FLAIR 上，最大概念匹配（MCM）對於遠 OOD 的 AUROC 達到 76.4%，但對於如超廣角眼底影像等協變變化僅為 42.4%，實際上是隨機的。我們將此追溯到結構不匹配：在 softmax 空間中，協變變化的輸入與分佈內樣本無法區分，但在 VLM 嵌入空間中卻佔據不同的區域。為了利用這一未開發的信號，我們提出了 PROTON（基於原型的測試時在線 OOD 檢測），這是一個輕量級的事後模塊，從高信心的測試預測中維護在線原型庫，並通過流級變異統計自適應地融合原型距離與 MCM 評分，無需模型修改、訓練數據或提示工程。在眼科基準 FLAIR + FIVES 上，PROTON 在協變變化上將 MCM 提升了 +23.9 AUROC，在語義變化上提升了 +8.8，在遠 OOD 上提升了 +8.1，使其成為唯一能在不使用層次提示或標記數據的情況下改善所有三者的零樣本方法。代碼可在 https://github.com/GenMI-Lab/PROTON 獲得，項目頁面可在 https://genmi-lab.github.io/PROTON 獲得。

##### **Neurosymbolic Clinical Trial Matching via LLM-Driven Abduction and Logical Verification**
2606.20895v1 by Baiyang Qu, Leonardo Ranaldi, Xi Wang, Marco Valentino

Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising path to automate Clinical Trial Matching (CTM), but still struggle with the deterministic verification required for complex eligibility criteria. Conversely, purely symbolic methods provide formal rigour but break down when faced with incomplete patient records and noisy clinical evidence. To bridge this gap, we investigate a hybrid framework for CTM combining LLMs with logical verification. In particular, we introduce an abductive neurosymbolic CTM framework (αNeSy-CTM), which leverages the linguistic and world knowledge in LLMs to support reasoning over noisy and underspecified clinical text. Extensive evaluation demonstrates that αNeSy-CTM substantially outperforms standalone LLM baselines, achieving up to 30% relative improvement over zero-shot baselines. In addition, our analyses confirm the impact of abductive reasoning on CTM, with αNeSy-CTM exhibiting improved accuracy, specificity, and robustness over a non-abductive neurosymbolic setting. Furthermore, αNeSy-CTM and Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning prove highly complementary, highlighting the potential for a hybrid routing policy. Ultimately, this paper demonstrates the impact of neurosymbolic methods for automating CTM, providing a path toward the next generation of auditable, LLM-driven clinical applications.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）為自動化臨床試驗匹配（CTM）提供了一條有希望的途徑，但在處理複雜的資格標準所需的確定性驗證時仍然面臨挑戰。相反，純符號方法提供了形式上的嚴謹性，但在面對不完整的病歷和嘈雜的臨床證據時會崩潰。為了彌補這一差距，我們研究了一個結合LLMs與邏輯驗證的CTM混合框架。特別是，我們介紹了一個推理神經符號CTM框架（αNeSy-CTM），該框架利用LLMs中的語言和世界知識來支持對嘈雜和不明確的臨床文本進行推理。廣泛的評估顯示，αNeSy-CTM的表現顯著優於獨立的LLM基準，實現了相對於零樣本基準高達30%的改進。此外，我們的分析確認了推理對CTM的影響，αNeSy-CTM在準確性、特異性和穩健性方面優於非推理神經符號設置。此外，αNeSy-CTM和思維鏈（CoT）推理被證明是高度互補的，突顯了混合路由策略的潛力。最終，本文展示了神經符號方法在自動化CTM中的影響，為下一代可審核的、以LLM驅動的臨床應用提供了道路。

##### **Machine Learning Classification of Cryopathy Syndromes: A Comprehensive Comparative Study**
2606.20874v1 by Nataliya Shakhovska, Valentyna Chopyak, Ivan Izonin, Vira Haievska

Cryopathy syndromes are difficult to classify because laboratory patterns often overlap across diagnostic categories, while some diagnoses are rare. This makes routine interpretation of cryoglobulin-related tests challenging and increases dependence on expert judgment. The aim of this study was to develop and compare machine learning approaches for automated classification of cryopathy syndromes from laboratory data and to identify a practical strategy for clinical decision support. Methods: We analysed laboratory records from 2,686 patients assigned to 14 diagnostic categories. The dataset included demographic variables, cryoglobulin measurements, precipitation tests, and hemagglutinin and hemolysin titers. Data preprocessing included cleaning, encoding, imputation, normalization, and construction of clinically informed interaction features. We evaluated 12 modelling strategies, including Random Forest, Gradient Boosted Trees, Multi-Layer Perceptron, soft-voting ensembles, class balancing with Synthetic Minority Over-sampling Technique, hierarchical classification, period-aware models, targeted binary classifiers, and probability calibration. Performance was assessed using stratified train-test evaluation and stratified 5-fold cross-validation. The main metrics were macro-averaged F1 score, accuracy, Top-3 accuracy, and expected calibration error. The overall task proved difficult because of marked class imbalance and clinical overlap between diagnoses. The best multiclass performance was achieved by a soft-voting ensemble of Random Forest and Gradient Boosted Trees. Cross-validation confirmed stable performance for the balanced Random Forest model. Tree-based methods consistently outperformed the neural network model. Feature engineering improved discrimination, and the most informative predictors were derived cryoglobulin-based interaction features.

摘要：冷病綜合症難以分類，因為實驗室模式在診斷類別之間經常重疊，而某些診斷則較為罕見。這使得對與冷球蛋白相關的檢測結果的常規解讀變得具有挑戰性，並增加了對專家判斷的依賴。這項研究的目的是開發和比較機器學習方法，以自動化從實驗室數據中對冷病綜合症的分類，並確定一種實用的臨床決策支持策略。方法：我們分析了來自2,686名患者的實驗室記錄，這些患者被分配到14個診斷類別。數據集包括人口統計變數、冷球蛋白測量、沉澱測試以及血凝素和溶血素的滴度。數據預處理包括清理、編碼、插補、正規化和臨床知識驅動的交互特徵構建。我們評估了12種建模策略，包括隨機森林、梯度提升樹、多層感知器、軟投票集成、使用合成少數類過採樣技術的類別平衡、分層分類、考慮時間的模型、目標二元分類器和概率校準。性能評估使用分層訓練-測試評估和分層5折交叉驗證。主要指標為宏平均F1分數、準確率、Top-3準確率和期望校準誤差。由於明顯的類別不平衡和診斷之間的臨床重疊，整體任務證明是困難的。最佳的多類別性能是通過隨機森林和梯度提升樹的軟投票集成實現的。交叉驗證確認了平衡隨機森林模型的穩定性能。基於樹的方法始終優於神經網絡模型。特徵工程提高了區分度，最具信息性的預測因子是基於冷球蛋白的交互特徵。

##### **Translating Inference-Time Control to Radiology Vision-Language Models: Activation Steering for Pneumonia Classification on Chest X-rays**
2606.20852v1 by Eduardo Moreno Judice de Mattos Farina, Mateus A. Esmeraldo, Felipe Akio Matsuoka, Paulo Eduardo de Aguiar Kuriki, Felipe Campos Kitamura

Inference-time engineering can alter model behavior without fine-tuning. However, its utility for improving diagnostic performance in medical vision-language models (VLMs) remains unclear. We aim to evaluate whether Contrastive Activation Addition (CAA) can improve pneumonia classification in chest radiograph VLMs without updating model weights. Three frozen chest radiograph VLMs (MedGemma-4B-IT, NV-Reason-CXR-3B, and CheXOne-3B) were evaluated on the public Kermany pneumonia test set. Classification was based on the logits of the tokens Yes and No under a binary prompt. Steering vectors included a 30-pair answer-bias control, a 30-pair pneumonia text contrast, and an image-conditioned contrast derived from 30 pneumonia and 30 normal development images. A deterministic 200-image development set was used for layer and scale selection (100 images) and threshold calibration (100 images). Performance was assessed using ROC-AUC, PR-AUC, F1 score, threshold analyses, reverse-vector controls, random-vector controls, and conditional bootstrap confidence intervals. Fixed-threshold F1 improvements were frequently observed but did not consistently indicate improved diagnostic performance. For MedGemma-4B-IT. NV-Reason-CXR-3B showed the strongest benefit: calibrated F1 improved from 0.7692 in the zero-shot setting to 0.8619 with pneumonia-text steering and to 0.8727 with image-conditioned steering. For CheXOne-3B, pneumonia-text steering increased calibrated F1 from 0.8528 to 0.8666, although the confidence interval crossed zero. On this public pneumonia benchmark, CAA substantially altered prediction score distributions and operating characteristics without fine-tuning. Meaningful performance gains were observed in one of three evaluated VLMs, suggesting that activation steering may serve as a lightweight approach for adapting medical VLM behavior.

摘要：推理時間工程可以在不進行微調的情況下改變模型行為。然而，它在改善醫療視覺-語言模型（VLMs）診斷性能方面的效用仍不明確。我們旨在評估對比激活添加（CAA）是否能在不更新模型權重的情況下改善胸部X光VLMs中的肺炎分類。三個凍結的胸部X光VLMs（MedGemma-4B-IT、NV-Reason-CXR-3B和CheXOne-3B）在公開的Kermany肺炎測試集上進行了評估。分類基於二元提示下的令牌“是”和“否”的logits。引導向量包括30對答案偏差控制、30對肺炎文本對比以及從30張肺炎和30張正常發展圖像中衍生的圖像條件對比。一個確定性的200張圖像開發集被用於層和比例選擇（100張圖像）及閾值校準（100張圖像）。性能評估使用ROC-AUC、PR-AUC、F1分數、閾值分析、反向向量控制、隨機向量控制和條件自助信賴區間。固定閾值的F1改進經常被觀察到，但並未一致地指示出改善的診斷性能。對於MedGemma-4B-IT，NV-Reason-CXR-3B顯示出最強的好處：經校準的F1從零樣本設置的0.7692提高到使用肺炎文本引導的0.8619，並在圖像條件引導下提高到0.8727。對於CheXOne-3B，肺炎文本引導將經校準的F1從0.8528提高到0.8666，儘管信賴區間跨越了零。在這個公開的肺炎基準上，CAA顯著改變了預測分數分佈和運行特性，而無需微調。在三個評估的VLMs中，觀察到有意義的性能提升，這表明激活引導可能作為一種輕量級的方法來調整醫療VLM的行為。

##### **B[FM]$^2$: Brain Foundation Model via Flow Matching with SplitUNet**
2606.20812v1 by Jaedong Hwang, Kathleen Zhang, Wei Dai, Konstantinos Kontras, Maarten Vanmarcke, Maarten De Vos, Ila Fiete, Paul Pu Liang

EEG foundation models can learn generalizable representations from large-scale EEG corpora to enable single-backbone transfer across diverse clinical and brain-computer interface tasks. Existing models typically discretize the continuous multi-channel EEG waveform into patches or codebook tokens and train a transformer with masked self-supervision. Recognizing that this discretization fragments continuous brain rhythms and obscures fine-grained temporal dynamics, we present B[FM]$^2$(Brain Foundation Model via Flow Matching), whose inductive bias aligns with the data by pretraining directly on the raw signal using continuous-time flow matching without patches, tokenization, or masking. However, multi-channel EEG signals pose an architectural challenge for flow matching: time is densely sampled and highly autocorrelated (thousands of timepoints), while the electrode axis is short (tens of channels) at distinct scalp positions. To address this time-electrode asymmetry, we introduce SplitUNet, a velocity network that factorizes each block into separate 1D temporal and 1D electrode convolutions and downsamples only along time, preserving electrode topology throughout the hierarchy. B[FM]$^2$ sets a new state of the art on 7 of 9 standard downstream EEG classification tasks, using a pretraining budget of only 36,895 segments ($\approx$ 307h), 1-2 orders of magnitude ($\approx$ 30x) less than required by existing EEG foundation models. Further, it generates synthetic EEGs that two board-certified neurologists cannot distinguish from brain data (Cohen's $κ=$ -0.096). https://jd730.github.io/projects/BFM2

摘要：EEG 基礎模型可以從大規模 EEG 資料庫中學習可泛化的表示，以實現跨多樣臨床和腦-電腦介面任務的單一骨幹轉移。現有模型通常將連續的多通道 EEG 波形離散化為補丁或代碼本標記，並使用遮蔽自我監督訓練Transformer。認識到這種離散化會破壞連續的腦節律並模糊細微的時間動態，我們提出了 B[FM]$^2$（通過流匹配的腦基礎模型），其歸納偏差通過直接在原始信號上進行預訓練來與數據對齊，使用連續時間流匹配而不需要補丁、標記化或遮蔽。然而，多通道 EEG 信號對流匹配提出了架構挑戰：時間密集取樣且高度自相關（數千個時間點），而電極軸在不同的頭皮位置上則較短（數十個通道）。為了解決這種時間-電極不對稱，我們引入了 SplitUNet，一種速度網絡，將每個區塊分解為獨立的 1D 時間和 1D 電極卷積，並僅沿時間進行下採樣，保留整個層級中的電極拓撲。B[FM]$^2$ 在 9 個標準下游 EEG 分類任務中的 7 個任務上創造了新的技術標杆，使用的預訓練預算僅為 36,895 段（約 307 小時），比現有的 EEG 基礎模型所需的少 1-2 個數量級（約 30 倍）。此外，它生成的合成 EEG 使兩位董事認證的神經科醫生無法與腦數據區分開來（Cohen's $κ=$ -0.096）。 https://jd730.github.io/projects/BFM2

#### Abstracts
##### **Mapping Political-Elite Networks in Europe with a Multilingual Joint Entity-Relation Extraction Pipeline**
2606.27347v1 by Kirill Solovev, Jana Lasser

Whether political elites organise into rent-seeking coalitions that capture public resources or civic networks that sustain governance is a central question in comparative politics. Yet observing these complex, informal, and adversarial ties at scale has historically required intensive manual coding, while automated text-as-data methods have largely been limited to simple co-occurrence. Recent large language model (LLM) approaches offer a path forward but often rely on proprietary APIs, lack cross-lingual capability, and struggle with scalable entity resolution. We present a modular, fully open-weight pipeline for multilingual joint entity-relation extraction that builds signed, temporal knowledge graphs from massive unstructured news corpora. It combines span-based named-entity recognition (NER) with a three-stage linking cascade mapping mentions to language-independent Wikidata identifiers; a high-throughput, ontology-constrained mixture-of-experts model then uses guided decoding to extract directed, signed relationships grounded in a domain ontology. A full-coverage spot-check against a 3491-relation gold standard shows high textual correctness (68.2% strict to 93.7% lenient). Two large-scale case studies validate the pipeline against the public record. In Austria, it reconstructs a political party's complete lifecycle, dating internal fractures and tracking personnel into successor factions and court convictions. In a Polish corpus, it uncovers the overlapping economic and governance networks of state-enterprise patronage, alongside the structurally balanced, signed conflict network of the polarized Civic Platform (Platforma Obywatelska, PO)--Law and Justice (Prawo i Sprawiedliwość, PiS) duopoly. By bridging raw multilingual text and structured relational data, our framework provides a robust, replicable foundation for cross-national empirical computational social science.

摘要：政治精英是否組織成捕捉公共資源的租金尋求聯盟或維持治理的公民網絡，是比較政治中的一個核心問題。<lb/>然而，在大規模觀察這些複雜的、非正式的和對抗性的聯繫歷史上，通常需要密集的手動編碼，而自動化的文本數據方法在很大程度上僅限於簡單的共現分析。<lb/>最近的大型語言模型（LLM）方法提供了一條前進的道路，但通常依賴於專有的API，缺乏跨語言能力，並且在可擴展的實體解析上面臨挑戰。<lb/>我們提出了一個模組化的、完全開放權重的多語言聯合實體-關係提取管道，該管道從大量非結構化新聞語料庫中構建簽名的、時間性的知識圖譜。<lb/>它將基於跨度的命名實體識別（NER）與三階段的鏈接級聯相結合，將提及映射到與語言無關的維基數據標識符；然後，一個高通量、受本體約束的專家混合模型使用引導解碼來提取基於領域本體的有向、簽名關係。<lb/>對3491個關係金標準的全面覆蓋抽查顯示出高文本正確性（68.2% 嚴格到 93.7% 寬鬆）。<lb/>兩個大規模案例研究驗證了該管道與公共記錄的一致性。在奧地利，它重建了一個政黨的完整生命周期，追溯內部裂痕並追蹤人員進入繼承派系和法院定罪。<lb/>在一個波蘭語料庫中，它揭示了國有企業贊助的重疊經濟和治理網絡，以及結構平衡的、簽名的兩極化公民平台（Platforma Obywatelska, PO）--法律與正義（Prawo i Sprawiedliwość, PiS）雙頭壟斷的衝突網絡。<lb/>通過橋接原始多語言文本和結構化關係數據，我們的框架為跨國實證計算社會科學提供了一個穩健、可複製的基礎。

##### **LMs as Task-Specific Knowledge Bases: An Interpretability Analysis**
2606.27237v1 by Amit Elhelo, Amir Globerson, Mor Geva

Language models (LMs) capture large amounts of factual knowledge applicable to a wide range of tasks, motivating the view of their parameters as a knowledge base. An important property of knowledge bases is that different queries for the same fact return consistent results, drawing on a single source of truth. We investigate whether LMs satisfy this property through behavioral and mechanistic analyses. Our results suggest that they encode knowledge in a task-specific manner. Behaviorally, facts acquired on one task frequently fail to co-emerge on others during training. Parameter localization experiments suggest a mechanistic explanation, revealing distinct parameter subsets underlying different tasks for the same fact. Finally, we show that chain-of-thought reasoning draws part of its effectiveness from engaging task-specific parameters beyond those tied to the evaluation task. Our findings suggest that what the model knows and how it is asked are intertwined in parameter space, undermining the "knowledge base" analogy and carrying implications for the reliability and controllability of factual knowledge in LMs.

摘要：語言模型（LMs）捕捉大量適用於廣泛任務的事實知識，這使得將其參數視為知識庫的觀點得以成立。知識庫的一個重要特性是，對於同一事實的不同查詢會返回一致的結果，依賴於單一的真實來源。我們通過行為和機理分析來研究 LMs 是否滿足這一特性。我們的結果表明，它們以任務特定的方式編碼知識。在行為上，在一個任務上獲得的事實在訓練期間經常無法在其他任務上共同出現。參數定位實驗提供了一種機理解釋，揭示了對於同一事實，不同任務所依賴的不同參數子集。最後，我們展示了思維鏈推理的有效性部分來自於參與任務特定參數的運用，這些參數超出了與評估任務相關的參數。我們的發現表明，模型所知的內容和提問的方式在參數空間中是交織在一起的，這削弱了“知識庫”類比的有效性，並對 LMs 中事實知識的可靠性和可控性帶來影響。

##### **From Celebrities to Anyone: Characterizing AI Nudification Content, Technology, and Community Dynamics on 4chan**
2606.27234v1 by Chi Cui, Yixin Wu, Yang Zhang

AI nudification uses generative models to create synthetic non-consensual sexually explicit imagery (SNEACI) of real individuals. Prior work has examined dedicated nudification platforms and model repositories, finding that most targets are female celebrities. However, the anonymous content community, where SNEACI is actively requested, generated, and exchanged, remains unexplored. In this work, we present a large-scale study of AI nudification in the wild, identifying 24,105 SNEACI items. We find a significant shift in target demographics: non-celebrity individuals now account for 55.8\% of targets, compared to only 4.7\% in prior studies, indicating that AI nudification has expanded from targeting public figures to increasingly harming individuals within users' own social circles. Meanwhile, open-source models dominate production, with Stable Diffusion family generating 42.7\% of images and Wan generating 66.5\% of videos, all driven by thousands of shared fine-tuned models and accessible tutorials. Yet the ecosystem runs on a small cohort of active producers, with the most prolific producing 780 items, drives community engagement, shapes target demographics, and disseminates technical knowledge that lowers barriers for new producers. Our work provides an empirical understanding of how AI nudification operates in the wild, revealing the mechanisms that sustain this ecosystem and highlighting the urgent need for interventions in platform governance, technical safeguards, and affected individual protection.

摘要：AI 裸露化使用生成模型創建真實個體的合成非自願性露骨影像 (SNEACI)。先前的研究考察了專門的裸露化平台和模型庫，發現大多數目標是女性名人。然而，匿名內容社區——SNEACI 在此社區中被積極請求、生成和交換——仍然未被探索。在這項工作中，我們呈現了一項關於 AI 裸露化的廣泛研究，識別出 24,105 件 SNEACI 物品。我們發現目標人口統計出現顯著變化：非名人個體現在佔目標的 55.8\%，而先前研究僅為 4.7\%，這表明 AI 裸露化已經從針對公眾人物擴展到越來越多地傷害用戶自身社交圈內的個體。同時，開源模型主導了生產，Stable Diffusion 系列生成了 42.7\% 的影像，而 Wan 則生成了 66.5\% 的視頻，這一切都是由數千個共享的微調模型和可訪問的教程驅動的。然而，生態系統依賴於一小部分活躍的生產者，其中最具生產力的生產了 780 件物品，推動了社區參與，塑造了目標人口統計，並傳播降低新生產者門檻的技術知識。我們的工作提供了對 AI 裸露化在實際運作中如何運行的實證理解，揭示了支撐這一生態系統的機制，並突顯了在平台治理、技術保障和受影響個體保護方面進行干預的迫切需求。

##### **Bridging Talk and Thought: Understanding Dialogue Dynamics Across Collaborative Problem-Solving Contexts**
2606.27233v1 by Zhengyuan Liu, Stella Xin Yin, Min-Yen Kan, Nancy F. Chen

We present a conceptual framework for analyzing dialogue in collaborative problem-solving contexts, with an emphasis on the emerging dynamics of human-AI and multi-agent collaboration. As intelligent systems become active agents capable of autonomous reasoning and strategic cooperation, understanding the dialogic interaction during collaborative problem solving is increasingly important for optimizing and evaluating such partnerships. Our framework addresses key limitations in current analytical approaches through a hierarchical two-layer coding scheme that integrates cognitive and non-cognitive problem solving with metacognitive regulatory mechanisms. ##### **Forecasting With LLMs: Improved Generalization Through Feature Steering**
2606.27199v1 by Humzah Merchant, Bradford Levy

Successful forecasting involves identifying patterns between historical and future states of the world which generalize to future observations. We apply LLMs to a variety of forecasting tasks and inspect their internal states using sparse autoencoders to understand whether they appear to rely on time-specific pieces of knowledge versus generalizable patterns. Our analyses identify features associated with both time-aware reasoning and look-ahead-biased reasoning. We then apply the LLMs to an entirely different domain and intervene on these features. We find that amplifying time-awareness features substantially reduces look-ahead bias on forecasting prompts while preserving general reasoning performance. In contrast, steering the candidate look-ahead-bias features does not produce an effect. These results suggest that interpretable temporal features can be used to causally shift LLMs toward more historically grounded reasoning.

摘要：成功的預測涉及識別歷史與未來世界狀態之間的模式，這些模式可以推廣到未來的觀察中。<lb/>我們將大型語言模型（LLMs）應用於各種預測任務，並使用稀疏自編碼器檢查它們的內部狀態，以了解它們是否依賴於特定時間的知識片段，而不是可推廣的模式。<lb/>我們的分析識別了與時間感知推理和前瞻性偏見推理相關的特徵。<lb/>然後，我們將LLMs應用於完全不同的領域，並對這些特徵進行干預。<lb/>我們發現，放大時間感知特徵顯著減少了預測提示上的前瞻性偏見，同時保持了一般推理性能。<lb/>相反，調整候選的前瞻性偏見特徵並未產生效果。<lb/>這些結果表明，可解釋的時間特徵可以用來因果性地將LLMs引導向更具歷史根基的推理。

##### **A Process Harness for Uplifting Legacy Workflows to Agentic BPM: Design and Realization in CUGA FLO**
2606.27188v1 by Fabiana Fournier, Lior Limonad

We introduce the process harness, a new mechanism for uplifting legacy workflows into Agentic Business Process Management (Agentic BPM) without replacing the underlying workflow engine. A process harness places a policy-governed agentic layer around a deterministic workflow engine, intercepting designated control points to contribute reasoning, adaptation, and oversight while the engine retains structural authority over the process. To define the process harness rigorously, we develop the Task-Decision-Flow (TDF) model, specifying both its data schema and its execution semantics. TDF decomposes LLM reasoning across three policy-governed agent types: a TaskAgent for knowledge-intensive task execution, a DecisionAgent for per-case gateway routing, and a FlowAgent that governs runtime flow adaptation through a principled hook mechanism. Each agent reasons within an explicit policy drawn from the process FRAME, the aggregate policy set governing all LLM calls in the system. We then present CUGA FLO as the design and implementation realization of the TDF model, and demonstrate it on a loan approval workflow that exercises all three agent types and hook-driven regulatory override. The process harness uniquely reconciles imperative requirements, realized through deterministic workflow execution that enforces structural compliance, with normative requirements, realized through policy-framed agentic autonomy invoked at designated control points wherever the process demands it.

摘要：我們介紹過程工具，這是一種新的機制，用於將傳統工作流程提升至代理商業流程管理（Agentic BPM），而無需替換底層工作流程引擎。過程工具在確定性工作流程引擎周圍放置了一個政策治理的代理層，攔截指定的控制點，以提供推理、適應和監督，同時引擎保持對過程的結構權威。為了嚴謹地定義過程工具，我們開發了任務-決策-流程（TDF）模型，具體說明了其數據架構和執行語義。TDF 在三種政策治理的代理類型之間分解 LLM 推理：一個用於知識密集型任務執行的 TaskAgent、一個用於逐案網關路由的 DecisionAgent，以及一個通過原則性掛鉤機制治理運行時流程適應的 FlowAgent。每個代理都在從過程 FRAME 中提取的明確政策內進行推理，該政策集是治理系統中所有 LLM 調用的綜合政策集。然後，我們展示 CUGA FLO 作為 TDF 模型的設計和實現實現，並在一個貸款批准工作流程中演示，該流程運用所有三種代理類型和基於掛鉤的監管覆蓋。過程工具獨特地調和了強制性要求，通過確定性工作流程執行來實現結構合規性，與規範性要求，通過在過程要求的指定控制點調用的政策框架代理自主性來實現。

##### **Efficient foundation decoders for fault-tolerant quantum computing**
2606.27119v1 by Ge Yan, Shanchuan Li, Shiyi Xiao, Pengyue Ma, Hanyan Cao, Feng Pan, Yuxuan Du

Foundation decoders, a class of high-capacity neural decoders, are leading candidates for fault-tolerant quantum computing, with accurate and efficient decoding at large code distances. However, their construction often faces a steep scaling barrier, as larger code distances rapidly amplify the cost of syndrome generation and neural optimization. To address this bottleneck, here we devise neural transfer unification (NTU), a unified framework for efficient foundation decoders. A central feature of NTU is its ability to align decoding tasks across code distances via algebraic structures shared by scalable code families, which enables knowledge learned on smaller codes to accelerate large-scale decoder training. We instantiate NTU as NTU-Transformer, a transformer-based neural decoder tailored for planar surface codes and bivariate bicycle codes. For planar surface codes under circuit-level noise, NTU-Transformer outperforms correlation-aware matching on the $[\![361,1,19]\!]$ code and further scales to the $[\![625,1,25]\!]$ code, where it exceeds standard matching through transfer adaptation. For the bivariate bicycle code with $[\![72,12,6]\!]$, it surpasses Relay-BP in the low-physical-error regime. These results establish our proposal as a scalable route to amortized cross-distance training of foundation decoders for fault-tolerant quantum processors.

摘要：基礎解碼器，一類高容量神經解碼器，是容錯量子計算的主要候選者，能在大碼距下進行準確且高效的解碼。然而，它們的構建往往面臨嚴峻的擴展障礙，因為更大的碼距迅速增加了綜合生成和神經優化的成本。為了解決這一瓶頸，我們在此設計了神經轉移統一（NTU），這是一個高效基礎解碼器的統一框架。NTU的一個核心特徵是其能夠通過可擴展碼族共享的代數結構來對齊不同碼距的解碼任務，這使得在較小碼上學到的知識能加速大規模解碼器的訓練。我們將NTU具體化為NTU-Transformer，一種基於Transformer的神經解碼器，專為平面表面碼和雙變量自行車碼量身定制。在電路級噪聲下的平面表面碼中，NTU-Transformer在$[\![361,1,19]\!]$碼上超越了考慮相關性的匹配，並進一步擴展到$[\![625,1,25]\!]$碼，在那裡它通過轉移適應超越了標準匹配。對於$[\![72,12,6]\!]$的雙變量自行車碼，它在低物理錯誤範疇中超越了Relay-BP。這些結果確立了我們的提議作為一條可擴展的路徑，實現基礎解碼器在容錯量子處理器上的跨距訓練。

##### **NuclearQAv2: A Structured Benchmark for Evaluating Domain-Science Competence in Large Language Models**
2606.27047v1 by Henry Shaowu Yuchi, Michal Kucer, Benjamin H. Sims, Selma Peterson, Emily Taylor

Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance across a wide range of tasks, but ensuring their reliability in highly technical domains remains a significant challenge. In nuclear engineering, problem solving often requires not only factual knowledge but also quantitative reasoning and conceptual understanding. To address the need for systematic evaluation in this domain, we introduce NuclearQAv2, a benchmark for assessing LLMs on nuclear engineering knowledge. The benchmark comprises approximately 1,240 question-answer pairs spanning three categories: boolean, numeric, and verbal. NuclearQAv2 is constructed using a hybrid pipeline that combines expert-authored questions, existing datasets, and LLM-assisted generation from domain-specific technical corpora. By leveraging structured prompting for both automated question generation and response evaluation, the proposed framework enables scalable benchmark construction and evaluation. We evaluate a diverse set of LLMs using NuclearQAv2 and observe substantial performance differences across task types. While the models generally perform well on factual questions, quantitative reasoning and conceptual understanding remain considerably more challenging. These results highlight the importance of multi-faceted evaluation frameworks and establish NuclearQAv2 as a scalable benchmark for assessing LLM capabilities in technical domains.
